I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Using `binding_array` should require an enable extension
Naga's WGSL front end requires a directive like `enable wgpu_mesh_shader;` or `enable wgpu_ray_query;` to use WGPU-specific features like mesh shaders or ray tracing, but nothing to use `binding_array`. It would be more consistent to require `enable wgpu_binding_array;`.

</pr_description>

    11	#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Eq, PartialEq)]
    12	pub(crate) struct EnableExtensions {

    21	    wgpu_cooperative_matrix: bool,

   159	            _ => return Err(Box::new(Error::UnknownEnableExtension(span, word))),

   161	    }

    24	/// State for constructing an AST expression.
    25	///
    26	/// Not to be confused with [`lower::ExpressionContext`], which is for producing
    27	/// Naga IR from the AST we produce here.
    28	///
    29	/// [`lower::ExpressionContext`]: super::lower::ExpressionContext
    30	struct ExpressionContext<'input, 'temp, 'out> {
    31	    /// The [`TranslationUnit::expressions`] arena to which we should contribute
    32	    /// expressions.
    33	    ///
    34	    /// [`TranslationUnit::expressions`]: ast::TranslationUnit::expressions
    35	    expressions: &'out mut Arena<ast::Expression<'input>>,
    36	
    37	    /// A map from identifiers in scope to the locals/arguments they represent.
    38	    ///
    39	    /// The handles refer to the [`locals`] arena; see that field's
    40	    /// documentation for details.
    41	    ///
    42	    /// [`locals`]: ExpressionContext::locals
    43	    local_table: &'temp mut SymbolTable<&'input str, Handle<ast::Local>>,
    44	
    45	    /// Local variable and function argument arena for the function we're building.
    46	    ///
    47	    /// Note that the [`ast::Local`] here is actually a zero-sized type. This
    48	    /// `Arena`'s only role is to assign a unique `Handle` to each local
    49	    /// identifier, and track its definition's span for use in diagnostics. All
    50	    /// the detailed information about locals - names, types, etc. - is kept in
    51	    /// the [`LocalDecl`] statements we parsed from their declarations. For
    52	    /// arguments, that information is kept in [`arguments`].
    53	    ///
    54	    /// In the AST, when an [`Ident`] expression refers to a local variable or
    55	    /// argument, its [`IdentExpr`] holds the referent's `Handle<Local>` in this
    56	    /// arena.
    57	    ///
    58	    /// During lowering, [`LocalDecl`] statements add entries to a per-function
    59	    /// table that maps `Handle<Local>` values to their Naga representations,
    60	    /// accessed via [`StatementContext::local_table`] and
    61	    /// [`LocalExpressionContext::local_table`]. This table is then consulted when
    62	    /// lowering subsequent [`Ident`] expressions.
    63	    ///
    64	    /// [`LocalDecl`]: ast::StatementKind::LocalDecl
    65	    /// [`arguments`]: ast::Function::arguments
    66	    /// [`Ident`]: ast::Expression::Ident
    67	    /// [`IdentExpr`]: ast::IdentExpr
    68	    /// [`StatementContext::local_table`]: super::lower::StatementContext::local_table
    69	    /// [`LocalExpressionContext::local_table`]: super::lower::LocalExpressionContext::local_table
    70	    locals: &'out mut Arena<ast::Local>,
    71	
    72	    /// Identifiers used by the current global declaration that have no local definition.
    73	    ///
    74	    /// This becomes the [`GlobalDecl`]'s [`dependencies`] set.
    75	    ///
    76	    /// Note that we don't know at parse time what kind of [`GlobalDecl`] the
    77	    /// name refers to. We can't look up names until we've seen the entire
    78	    /// translation unit.
    79	    ///
    80	    /// [`GlobalDecl`]: ast::GlobalDecl
    81	    /// [`dependencies`]: ast::GlobalDecl::dependencies
    82	    unresolved: &'out mut FastIndexSet<ast::Dependency<'input>>,
    83	}
    84	
    85	impl<'a> ExpressionContext<'a, '_, '_> {
    86	    fn parse_binary_op(
    87	        &mut self,
    88	        lexer: &mut Lexer<'a>,
    89	        classifier: impl Fn(Token<'a>) -> Option<crate::BinaryOperator>,
    90	        mut parser: impl FnMut(&mut Lexer<'a>, &mut Self) -> Result<'a, Handle<ast::Expression<'a>>>,
    91	    ) -> Result<'a, Handle<ast::Expression<'a>>> {
    92	        let start = lexer.start_byte_offset();
    93	        let mut accumulator = parser(lexer, self)?;
    94	        while let Some(op) = classifier(lexer.peek().0) {
    95	            let _ = lexer.next();
    96	            let left = accumulator;
    97	            let right = parser(lexer, self)?;
    98	            accumulator = self.expressions.append(
    99	                ast::Expression::Binary { op, left, right },
   100	                lexer.span_from(start),
   101	            );
   102	        }
   103	        Ok(accumulator)
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    fn declare_local(&mut self, name: ast::Ident<'a>) -> Result<'a, Handle<ast::Local>> {
   107	        let handle = self.locals.append(ast::Local, name.span);
   108	        if let Some(old) = self.local_table.add(name.name, handle) {
   109	            Err(Box::new(Error::Redefinition {
   110	                previous: self.locals.get_span(old),
   111	                current: name.span,
   112	            }))
   113	        } else {
   114	            Ok(handle)
   115	        }
   116	    }
   117	}

   120	///

     9	pub fn map_address_space<'a>(
    10	    word: &str,
    11	    span: Span,
    12	    enable_extensions: &EnableExtensions,
    13	) -> Result<'a, crate::AddressSpace> {
    14	    match word {
    15	        "private" => Ok(crate::AddressSpace::Private),
    16	        "workgroup" => Ok(crate::AddressSpace::WorkGroup),
    17	        "uniform" => Ok(crate::AddressSpace::Uniform),
    18	        "storage" => Ok(crate::AddressSpace::Storage {
    19	            access: crate::StorageAccess::default(),
    20	        }),
    21	        "immediate" => Ok(crate::AddressSpace::Immediate),
    22	        "function" => Ok(crate::AddressSpace::Function),
    23	        "task_payload" => {
    24	            enable_extensions.require(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuMeshShader, span)?;
    25	            Ok(crate::AddressSpace::TaskPayload)
    26	        }
    27	        "ray_payload" => {
    28	            if enable_extensions.contains(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayTracingPipeline) {
    29	                Ok(crate::AddressSpace::RayPayload)
    30	            } else {
    31	                Err(Box::new(Error::EnableExtensionNotEnabled {
    32	                    span,
    33	                    kind: ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayTracingPipeline.into(),
    34	                }))
    35	            }
    36	        }
    37	        "incoming_ray_payload" => {
    38	            if enable_extensions.contains(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayTracingPipeline) {
    39	                Ok(crate::AddressSpace::IncomingRayPayload)
    40	            } else {
    41	                Err(Box::new(Error::EnableExtensionNotEnabled {
    42	                    span,
    43	                    kind: ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayTracingPipeline.into(),
    44	                }))
    45	            }
    46	        }
    47	        _ => Err(Box::new(Error::UnknownAddressSpace(span))),
    48	    }
    49	}
    50	
    51	pub fn map_access_mode(word: &str, span: Span) -> Result<'_, crate::StorageAccess> {
    52	    match word {
    53	        "read" => Ok(crate::StorageAccess::LOAD),
    54	        "write" => Ok(crate::StorageAccess::STORE),
    55	        "read_write" => Ok(crate::StorageAccess::LOAD | crate::StorageAccess::STORE),
    56	        "atomic" => Ok(crate::StorageAccess::ATOMIC
    57	            | crate::StorageAccess::LOAD
    58	            | crate::StorageAccess::STORE),
    59	        _ => Err(Box::new(Error::UnknownAccess(span))),
    60	    }
    61	}

    64	    enable_extensions: &EnableExtensions,

    66	    span: Span,

   286	    /// Helper method which writes all the `enable` declarations
   287	    /// needed for a module.
   288	    fn write_enable_declarations(&mut self, module: &Module) -> BackendResult {
   289	        #[derive(Default)]
   290	        struct RequiredEnabled {
   291	            f16: bool,
   292	            dual_source_blending: bool,
   293	            clip_distances: bool,
   294	            mesh_shaders: bool,
   295	            primitive_index: bool,
   296	            cooperative_matrix: bool,
   297	            draw_index: bool,
   298	            ray_tracing_pipeline: bool,
   299	            per_vertex: bool,
   300	        }
   301	        let mut needed = RequiredEnabled {
   302	            mesh_shaders: module.uses_mesh_shaders(),
   303	            ..Default::default()
   304	        };
   305	
   306	        let check_binding = |binding: &crate::Binding, needed: &mut RequiredEnabled| match *binding
   307	        {
   308	            crate::Binding::Location {
   309	                blend_src: Some(_), ..
   310	            } => {
   311	                needed.dual_source_blending = true;
   312	            }
   313	            crate::Binding::BuiltIn(crate::BuiltIn::ClipDistances) => {
   314	                needed.clip_distances = true;
   315	            }
   316	            crate::Binding::BuiltIn(crate::BuiltIn::PrimitiveIndex) => {
   317	                needed.primitive_index = true;
   318	            }
   319	            crate::Binding::Location {
   320	                per_primitive: true,
   321	                ..
   322	            } => {
   323	                needed.mesh_shaders = true;
   324	            }
   325	            crate::Binding::Location {
   326	                interpolation: Some(crate::Interpolation::PerVertex),
   327	                ..
   328	            } => {
   329	                needed.per_vertex = true;
   330	            }
   331	            crate::Binding::BuiltIn(crate::BuiltIn::DrawIndex) => needed.draw_index = true,
   332	            crate::Binding::BuiltIn(

   334	                | crate::BuiltIn::NumRayInvocations
   335	                | crate::BuiltIn::InstanceCustomData
   336	                | crate::BuiltIn::GeometryIndex
   337	                | crate::BuiltIn::WorldRayOrigin
   338	                | crate::BuiltIn::WorldRayDirection
   339	                | crate::BuiltIn::ObjectRayOrigin

   345	            ) => {
   346	                needed.ray_tracing_pipeline = true;
   347	            }
   348	            _ => {}
   349	        };
   350	
   351	        // Determine which `enable` declarations are needed
   352	        for (_, ty) in module.types.iter() {
   353	            match ty.inner {

   357	                    needed.f16 |= scalar == crate::Scalar::F16;
   358	                }

   366	                }

   369	                }

   371	            }

   377	            }

  1040	///
  1041	/// For the first case, we use the supplied test case source verbatim (which
  1042	/// should not include the `enable` directive), and check for a parse error
  1043	/// matching the expected error message text. For the second case, we add the
  1044	/// `enable` directive to the supplied test case, and check for a validation
  1045	/// error matching the expected pattern.
  1046	///
  1047	/// The WGSL frontend is not the only way of producing Naga IR, and the
  1048	/// validator must reject an invalid module however produced. So it is important
  1049	/// that the validator check for missing capabilities. Checking missing
  1050	/// extensions in the frontend as well can produce better error messages or
  1051	/// simplify implementation of the frontend by eliminating some cases of invalid
  1052	/// programs earlier.
  1053	///
  1054	/// Multiple capabilities can be specified in the macro argument in the case
  1055	/// where any one of them grants access to a feature (e.g. `SUBGROUP` and
  1056	/// `SUBGROUP_BARRIER` for `subgroupBarrier`). When passing multiple capabilities,
  1057	/// all of the passed capabilities must be covered by the same enable-extension.
  1058	///
  1059	/// NOTE: The only reason we don't use a function for this is because we need to syntactically
  1060	/// re-use `$val_err_pat`.
  1061	///
  1062	/// The optional $other_caps argument at the end specifies capabilities that
  1063	/// allow, the shader or would change the error message if enabled, but do not
  1064	/// get enabled by the specified enable extension. This is only currently the
  1065	/// case for `acceleration_structures` which are enabled by both ray queries
  1066	/// and ray tracing pipelines.
  1067	macro_rules! check_extension_validation {
  1068	    ( $caps:expr, $source:expr, $parse_err:expr, $val_err_pat:pat $(, $other_caps:expr)? ) => {
  1069	        #[allow(unused_mut, unused_assignments)]
  1070	        let mut other_caps = naga::valid::Capabilities::empty();
  1071	        $(other_caps = $other_caps;)?
  1072	        let caps = $caps;
  1073	        let source = $source;
  1074	        let mut ext = None;
  1075	        for cap in caps.iter() {
  1076	            match cap.extension() {
  1077	                Some(this_ext) if ext.is_none() => ext = Some(this_ext),
  1078	                Some(this_ext) if ext.is_some_and(|ext| ext != this_ext) => {
  1079	                    panic!(
  1080	                        concat!(
  1081	                            "the capabilities {:?} in `check_extension_validation` ",
  1082	                            "are not all covered by the same extension ",
  1083	                            "(found both {:?} and {:?})",
  1084	                        ),
  1085	                        caps, ext, this_ext,
  1086	                    );
  1087	                }
  1088	                _ => {}
  1089	            }
  1090	        }
  1091	        let Some(ext) = ext else {
  1092	            panic!(
  1093	                concat!(
  1094	                    "None of the capabilities {:?} in `check_extension_validation` ",
  1095	                    "are associated with an extension. ",
  1096	                    "Use `check_validation!` to check validator behavior ",
  1097	                    "when there isn't a corresponding parse error.",
  1098	                ),
  1099	                caps
  1100	            );
  1101	        };
  1102	        let directive = format!(
  1103	            "enable {};",
  1104	            naga::front::wgsl::EnableExtension::Implemented(ext).to_ident()
  1105	        );
  1106	        assert!(
  1107	            !source.contains(&directive),
  1108	            "test case for `check_extension_validation!` should not contain the enable directive",
  1109	        );
  1110	
  1111	        // First check, for the expected WGSL parse error when extension is not enabled
  1112	        check(&source, $parse_err);
  1113	        let source_with_enable = format!("{directive}\n{source}");
  1114	        let module = match naga::front::wgsl::parse_str(&source_with_enable) {
  1115	            Ok(module) => module,
  1116	            Err(err) => {
  1117	                eprintln!("WGSL parse failed:");
  1118	                panic!("{}", err.emit_to_string(source));
  1119	            }
  1120	        };
  1121	
  1122	        // Second check, for the expected validation error when the capability is not present
  1123	        // Don't check with explicitly allowed caps, as certain things (currently just
  1124	        // `acceleration_structure`s) can be enabled by multiple extensions
  1125	        let error = naga::valid::Validator::new(naga::valid::ValidationFlags::all(), !(caps | other_caps))

   253	    /// Supported subgroup operations
   254	    #[cfg_attr(feature = "serialize", derive(serde::Serialize))]
   255	    #[cfg_attr(feature = "deserialize", derive(serde::Deserialize))]
   256	    #[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Default, Eq, PartialEq)]
   257	    pub struct SubgroupOperationSet: u8 {
   258	        /// Barriers
   259	        // Possibly elections, when that is supported.
   260	        // https://github.com/gfx-rs/wgpu/issues/6042#issuecomment-3272603431
   261	        // Contrary to what the name "basic" suggests, HLSL/DX12 support the
   262	        // other subgroup operations, but do not support subgroup barriers.
   263	        const BASIC = 1 << 0;
   264	        /// Any, All
   265	        const VOTE = 1 << 1;
   266	        /// reductions, scans
   267	        const ARITHMETIC = 1 << 2;
   268	        /// ballot, broadcast
   269	        const BALLOT = 1 << 3;
   270	        /// shuffle, shuffle xor
   271	        const SHUFFLE = 1 << 4;
   272	        /// shuffle up, down
   273	        const SHUFFLE_RELATIVE = 1 << 5;
   274	        // We don't support these operations yet
   275	        // /// Clustered
   276	        // const CLUSTERED = 1 << 6;
   277	        /// Quad supported
   278	        const QUAD_FRAGMENT_COMPUTE = 1 << 7;
   279	        // /// Quad supported in all stages
   280	        // const QUAD_ALL_STAGES = 1 << 8;
   281	    }
   282	}
   283	
   284	impl super::SubgroupOperation {
   285	    const fn required_operations(&self) -> SubgroupOperationSet {
   286	        use SubgroupOperationSet as S;
   287	        match *self {
   288	            Self::All | Self::Any => S::VOTE,
   289	            Self::Add | Self::Mul | Self::Min | Self::Max | Self::And | Self::Or | Self::Xor => {
   290	                S::ARITHMETIC
   291	            }
   292	        }
   293	    }
   294	}
   295	
   296	impl super::GatherMode {
   297	    const fn required_operations(&self) -> SubgroupOperationSet {
   298	        use SubgroupOperationSet as S;
   299	        match *self {
   300	            Self::BroadcastFirst | Self::Broadcast(_) => S::BALLOT,
   301	            Self::Shuffle(_) | Self::ShuffleXor(_) => S::SHUFFLE,
   302	            Self::ShuffleUp(_) | Self::ShuffleDown(_) => S::SHUFFLE_RELATIVE,
   303	            Self::QuadBroadcast(_) | Self::QuadSwap(_) => S::QUAD_FRAGMENT_COMPUTE,
   304	        }
   305	    }
   306	}

     8	/// Map [`wgt::Features`] and [`wgt::DownlevelFlags`] to [`naga::valid::Capabilities`].
     9	pub fn features_to_naga_capabilities(
    10	    features: wgt::Features,
    11	    downlevel: wgt::DownlevelFlags,
    12	) -> Caps {
    13	    let mut caps = Caps::empty();
    14	    caps.set(
    15	        Caps::IMMEDIATES,

    17	    );

   141	    /// Convert from a sentinel word in WGSL into its associated [`EnableExtension`], if possible.
   142	    pub(crate) fn from_ident(word: &str, span: Span) -> Result<'_, Self> {
   143	        Ok(match word {
   144	            Self::F16 => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::F16),
   145	            Self::CLIP_DISTANCES => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::ClipDistances),
   146	            Self::DUAL_SOURCE_BLENDING => {
   147	                Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::DualSourceBlending)

   149	            Self::MESH_SHADER => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuMeshShader),

   151	            Self::RAY_QUERY => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayQuery),
   152	            Self::RAY_QUERY_VERTEX_RETURN => {
   153	                Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayQueryVertexReturn)
   154	            }
   155	            Self::RAY_TRACING_PIPELINE => {
   156	                Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayTracingPipeline)
   157	            }

   163	            Self::PRIMITIVE_INDEX => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::PrimitiveIndex),
   164	            Self::PER_VERTEX => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::PerVertex),
   165	            _ => return Err(Box::new(Error::UnknownEnableExtension(span, word))),
   166	        })
   167	    }

   173	                ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuMeshShader => Self::MESH_SHADER,
   174	                ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuBindingArray => Self::BINDING_ARRAY,

   239	}

   241	impl ImplementedEnableExtension {
   242	    /// A slice of all variants of [`ImplementedEnableExtension`].
   243	    pub const VARIANTS: &'static [Self] = &[
   244	        Self::F16,
   245	        Self::DualSourceBlending,
   246	        Self::ClipDistances,
   247	        Self::WgpuMeshShader,
   248	        Self::WgpuBindingArray,
   249	        Self::WgpuRayQuery,
   250	        Self::WgpuRayQueryVertexReturn,
   251	        Self::WgpuRayTracingPipeline,
   252	        Self::WgpuCooperativeMatrix,
   253	        Self::DrawIndex,
   254	        Self::PrimitiveIndex,
   255	        Self::PerVertex,
   256	    ];
   257	
   258	    /// Returns slice of all variants of [`ImplementedEnableExtension`].
   259	    pub const fn all() -> &'static [Self] {
   260	        Self::VARIANTS
   261	    }
   262	
   263	    /// Returns the capability required for this enable extension.
   264	    pub const fn capability(self) -> crate::valid::Capabilities {
   265	        use crate::valid::Capabilities as C;
   266	        match self {
   267	            Self::F16 => C::SHADER_FLOAT16,
   268	            Self::DualSourceBlending => C::DUAL_SOURCE_BLENDING,
   269	            Self::ClipDistances => C::CLIP_DISTANCES,
   270	            Self::WgpuMeshShader => C::MESH_SHADER,
   271	            Self::WgpuBindingArray => C::empty(),
   272	            Self::WgpuRayQuery => C::RAY_QUERY,
   273	            Self::WgpuRayQueryVertexReturn => C::RAY_HIT_VERTEX_POSITION,
   274	            Self::WgpuCooperativeMatrix => C::COOPERATIVE_MATRIX,
   275	            Self::WgpuRayTracingPipeline => C::RAY_TRACING_PIPELINE,
   276	            Self::DrawIndex => C::DRAW_INDEX,
   277	            Self::PrimitiveIndex => C::PRIMITIVE_INDEX,
   278	            Self::PerVertex => C::PER_VERTEX,
   279	        }
   280	    }
